#Title history is mainly copied over from Oriental Empires. Unfortunately the title history doesn't go much past 1140 so after that I mainly just made sure to fill in vassals with whatever I had available/made up things where needed aka I made vassals dynastic. The hope would be that OE will eventually get to later dates as no CK2 mod has these later dates filled in with anything but made up characters themselves

#All eastern Steppe and Korea. Xia part of China is in 00_CENTRAL ASIA where the rest of Xia is
